#### ç ´åæ€§æ›´æ–°

- Table: é»˜è®¤æƒ…å†µä¸‹ `FilterMultiple=false`ï¼Œå†…ç½® Filter åˆ™ä¸æ˜¾ç¤º â€œ+â€ æŒ‰é’®ï¼Œå¦‚éœ€å¼€å¯åªéœ€è®¾ç½® â€œFilterMultiple=trueâ€ã€‚
- Input: åŸæ¥çš„ `Onkey*` API é‡å‘½åä¸º `OnKey*`ã€‚
- Modal

  - æ–¹æ³• `CreateConfirmAsync<TComponent, TComponentOptions, TResult>(ConfirmOptions config, TComponentOptions componentOptions);` è¿”å›å€¼ä» `Task<ConfirmRef<TResult>>` æ”¹ä¸º `Task<ConfirmResult>`ã€‚
  - ModalService.CreateComfirmAsync(...) çš„ `OnOk`ã€`OnCancel` ç­‰å§”æ‰˜è®¾ç½®ä»åŸæ¥çš„åœ¨ ConfirmRef æ”¹ä¸ºåœ¨ ConfirmOptions è®¾ç½®ï¼š
  
    ```cs
      var options = new ConfirmOptions<string>()
      {
         Title = "Confirm",
         Width = 350,
         Content = content,
         OnOpen = async () =>
         {
             Console.WriteLine("Open Confirm");
         },
         OnClose = async () =>
         {
             Console.WriteLine("Close Confirm");
         },
         OnCancel = async (result) =>
         {
             Console.WriteLine($"OnCancel:{result}");
         },
         OnOk = async (result) =>
         {
             Console.WriteLine($"OnOk:{result}");
         }
      };

      await ModalService.CreateConfirmAsync(options);
    ```

- Table : `RowTemplate` æ”¹ä¸º `ColumnDefinitions`ã€‚`RowTemplate` åŸæ¥ç”¨äº `Column` å®šä¹‰ï¼Œè¿™ä¸ªç‰ˆæœ¬ä¹‹åæ”¹ä¸ºç”¨äºå®šä¹‰è¡Œæ¨¡æ¿ã€‚
- ReuseTabs: `ReuseTabsRouteView` å’Œ `AuthorizeReuseTabsRouteView` å·²è¢«æ ‡è®°ä¸ºå¼ƒç”¨ã€‚ è¯·ç”¨`<CascadingValue Value="routeData">` åŒ…è£¹ `<RouteView>` æˆ– `<AuthorizeRouteView>`ã€‚
  
  å³ï¼š

  ```diff

    <Found Context="routeData">
  +   <CascadingValue Value="routeData">
        <RouteView RouteData="@routeData" DefaultLayout="@typeof(MainLayout)" />
  +   </CascadingValue>
    </Found>
    <NotFound>
        <LayoutView Layout="@typeof(MainLayout)">
            <p>Sorry, there's nothing at this address.</p>
        </LayoutView>
    </NotFound>
  </Router>
  ```
